msg:Objective evaluation. I think other reviews are basically fake.
I checked into the hotel at 12:30 last night. I thought the hotel was relatively new and the reviews were all clean. But when I opened the door and entered the room, there was a strong smell of formaldehyde, as if it had been closed for several days and couldn't be helped.
I called the front desk and they only said they could find me an air purifier.
I brought my one-and-a-half-year-old baby with me. The baby was very sleepy, and I couldn't sleep even if I turned on the machine at night. I just endured the stench that night.

There were also two vases with lids on the wooden cabinet at the elevator door. It looked like ***... I didn't take a picture. I was scared when I went in late at night, but I didn't get angry because I was afraid that the child would be scared. You can use your imagination.
